    FROM [Canteens] AS [c]
    WHERE [c].[Id] = @__canteenId_0
) AS [t]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [m].[Id], [m].[CanteenId], [m].[CategoryId], [m].[DailyMenuId], [m].[Description], [m].[Name], [m].[PictureURL], [m].[PortionId], [m].[Price], [c0].[Id] AS [Id0], [c0].[CategoryName], [p].[Id] AS [Id1], [p].[PortionName]
    FROM [Meals] AS [m]
    INNER JOIN [Categories] AS [c0] ON [m].[CategoryId] = [c0].[Id]
    INNER JOIN [Portions] AS [p] ON [m].[PortionId] = [p].[Id]
) AS [t0] ON [t].[Id] = [t0].[CanteenId]
ORDER BY [t].[Id], [t0].[Id], [t0].[Id0]
